ПРОИЗВОДСТВЕННАЯ БИБЛИЯ AWARA (Агенты 1-18)

==========================================
АГЕНТ №1: Свет Ра (Svet Ra)
==========================================

### Матрица: Vedic
**Image Prompt:** AWARA canonical avatar series, mystical high-fantasy portrait, semi-realistic, ultra-detailed, elegant sacred character design, game-ready avatar, centered composition, 1:1 portrait framing, bust or waist-up, clean readable silhouette, luminous skin, expressive eyes, subtle sacred mandala halo, refined symbolic costume, ornate but balanced details, rich spiritual atmosphere, soft volumetric light, cinematic glow, deep mystical background, consistent visual language across all characters, same rendering style, same quality level, same sacred design system, family resemblance between all avatars, immersive, intuitive, iconic, beautiful, no clutter. Свет Ра (Svet Ra), central solar consciousness, noble and androgynous male-presenting archetype, radiant golden-white aura, sun-crown halo, white-gold robes, sphere of living light. Translate the character through the Vedic matrix. Use sacred Indian-inspired symbolic aesthetics, subtle mandala geometry, lotus motifs, yantra-like halo. Negative prompt: text, caption, logo, watermark, low quality, blurry, deformed anatomy, extra fingers, extra arms, duplicate face, multiple characters, cropped head, bad eyes, distorted proportions, horror, grotesque, chaotic background, random sci-fi junk, parody, cartoonish exaggeration, low detail, muddy colors.
**Video Prompt:** Cinematic high-dynamic motion, sacred animation, subtle breathing, soft blinking, gentle movement of hair and fabric, floating particles of light, aura slowly pulsing, slight camera push-in, elegant magical motion, seamless loop, mystical and calm presence, heart-light pulsing, background shimmering with Vedic specific energy.
